(April 23rd)

The Wind and Rain Calamity in Xiangyuan

Changsha Dispatch: Since the beginning of spring in Xiangyuan, the weather has been unusually erratic, alternating between heat and cold. In recent days, it has been particularly oppressive and dry, almost like midsummer. On the 24th, around 2 AM, a sudden violent wind roared, accompanied by thunder and lightning and torrential rain, like ten thousand horses galloping. Most of the city's electricity and telephone lines were damaged. In one corner of the provincial capital, the losses on land and water were enormous. Numerous houses were blown down and boats overturned. The following is a detailed record of the investigations:

Land Losses: The losses on land were greater than those on the water. In the Eastern District, the entire roof of the rear building of the Demao Public Inn at No. 78 Luoxing Tian Lane collapsed, crushing to death Cai Yukun's seven-year-old daughter, Huaiying, and injuring his second daughter, Aizhong, a female worker named Zhong Luo, and Cai's wife, Luo, who suffered severe head injuries. All were sent to the public hospital for treatment. In the Southern District, Chen Chunqing, a small vendor selling dumplings at the Dung Wharf, was electrocuted by a broken power line. Also, the wall of the sales department of the Minle Grand Theater at Xinjiekou collapsed, injuring driver Ou Haiqing and apprentice Zhou Shaofang, who were both sent to Ren'ai Hospital for treatment. In the Western District, the building of the Songmao Machine Shop at No. 4 Fuqing Street completely collapsed, crushing apprentice Peng Changgeng to death and injuring helpers Zou Gaowu and Ren Sanyou, and apprentice Li Jinkai, all of whom were sent to Ren'ai Hospital for treatment. In the Northern District, the roof of Wang Yuntian's house at No. 5 Zhongfu Yuan collapsed, crushing to death his three-year-old grandson, Shengzheng, and his two-month-old infant, Cezheng. A portion of Cao Renshou's house at No. 29 Youpu Street was also blown down, injuring one person. A large maple tree at the Kalanjing Temple in Liufangling was blown down, landing on Hu Xichu's house at No. 74, fortunately without injuring anyone. In the commercial area, the roofs of the four-story Changjiang Hotel and the glass roof of the Maofeng Rice Mill were blown down into the street. At Yucai Middle School outside Liuyangmen, both dormitories and classrooms collapsed. At the same time, the heavy rain caused the dormitories to flood, turning them into ponds. More than 300 students could not sleep and were all complaining bitterly. Many fell ill due to the wind and rain. Four ancient trees inside the Finance Department and a large camphor tree with a one-foot circumference inside the Confucius Temple were uprooted, damaging several houses. Also, an ancient locust tree planted by Empress Dowager Cixi of the deposed Qing dynasty in the Changsha County government (said to have been planted by Cixi when she accompanied her father, Yulu, who was serving as the prefect of Changsha) was also uprooted, showing the force of the wind.

Water Losses: Due to the extremely strong winds at night and the rising spring tides, about twenty boats anchored in the provincial river had their anchors pulled, overturned, or collided and sank, mostly coal barges from Hengzhou. Whether anyone was injured is currently unknown. Along the river, many shanties had their thatched roofs blown off, leaving the residents with nowhere to live. They are currently being temporarily housed in the Waterside Temple by the Water and Land Police to prevent them from wandering. Water traffic in and out of the province was suspended for one day yesterday. Both wired and wireless communications were disrupted. The fine rain continues today and has not yet cleared (25th).

Northeastern China Actively Prepares Defenses in Luandong

Establishing a Temporary Luandong Garrison Headquarters

One Division and Two Brigades Ordered to Depart for Luan

Shenyang Dispatch: After Yan and Feng's rebellion, the attitude of Northeastern China has attracted much attention. Although Zhang Xueliang has convened a meeting of key figures from four provinces, hoping for peace, he is indeed sincere in supporting the central government. In the middle of this month, the "Tunan" steamship carried field artillery, machine guns, and other supplies from Yingkou to Ning. Preparations are now underway for a second batch of military supplies, with various types of ammunition scheduled to be shipped by the end of the month, currently being packed. Meanwhile, a decision has been made to actively fortify eastern Luanzhou, appointing Yu Xuezhong and Ji Jinchun as the overall commander and deputy commander of the temporary Luandong garrison, respectively. Yu came to Shenyang on the 15th to receive instructions and returned to Luanzhou on the 19th. Ji is stationed permanently in Yuzhou. The armored train and other units from Beida Camp, with over a hundred officers and soldiers and ten armored vehicles, were ordered to depart for Shanhaiguan on the 18th. The 1st Cavalry Division stationed in Shanhaiguan, the 4th Infantry Brigade stationed in Huanzhong, and the 20th Brigade stationed in Yixian were all ordered to prepare to depart for Luanzhou. A certain three regiments of the Jin Army stationed in Luanzhou are gathering vehicles at the Luanzhou Railway Station, preparing to return to Tangshan. The Shanhaiguan Railway Station has also placed numerous empty cars, dedicated to transport. Zhang Xueliang believes that Mongolia and Jehol, bordering Chahar, also need to be guarded. He ordered Tang Yulin to return to Jehol and prepare all matters related to defense. When Tang departed on the 19th, he received two million in military expenses. The defense of Funing and other places will be handled by the Jehol Army. The former Northeast Artillery has been reorganized, now consisting of three brigades and one division, with Zou Zuohua serving as the commander of the artillery division. Brigade commanders Qiao, Zhang, and Wang have already been announced. After official appointments are made, they will be distributed between Luandong, Jehol, and Suiyuan to strengthen defensive capabilities. (Zhenri News Agency)

Northeastern China's Methods for Settling Zhejiang Immigrants

Shenyang Dispatch: Due to continuous disasters and poor harvests in Zhejiang Province, the people are displaced and suffering. The chairman of the provincial government, Zhang Jingjiang, sent representative Li Guangyu to Shenyang to contact Commander Zhang Xueliang, requesting the immigration of 40,000 households, totaling 150,000 people, to Northeastern China for cultivation. Zhang submitted the matter to the Political Committee for discussion, and it was decided to first allow the immigration of 400 households (totaling over 3,000 people). After the Political Committee approved, it was handed over to the Liaoning Provincial Government for processing. The Provincial Government then convened various agencies and legal entities to discuss the matter together, deciding to assign them to various counties: 80 households to Shenyang County (5-6 people per household, both male and female), 50 households to Yingkou County, 50 households to Xinmin County, and 20-30 households each to Tie嶺 and other counties. After Zhejiang representative Li Guangyu telegraphed the number of immigrants to the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Zhejiang Province allocated 30,000 yuan in cash for travel expenses. They boarded ships on the 20th of this month and traveled north by sea. Shenyang County Magistrate Wang Jiarui, knowing that these immigrants are about to arrive in Shenyang, convened the heads of the Finance and Public Security Bureaus for an emergency meeting at 4 PM on the 21st to discuss settlement methods. It was decided that, as a first step, when these immigrants arrive in Shenyang, the Finance Bureau will allocate funds, and the Agricultural Association will send personnel to provide food and accommodation. Secondly, the 80 households allocated to Shenyang will be assessed by each Public Security Sub-bureau for wealthy households in the villages under their jurisdiction. Each household will settle one immigrant household, providing food and clothing, and the men will work for the wealthy households. After the paddy fields and the fields at Mentai in the west of the city are recovered, methods will be found to distribute them for cultivation. (April 23rd)

Establishment of the Liaoning Foreign Affairs Commissioner's Office

Shenyang Dispatch: After the Foreign Ministry's Liaoning Foreign Affairs Commissioner's Office was officially established on the first of this month, all the office's regulations and budgetary estimates have been drafted by Commissioner Wang Jinghuan and submitted to the Provincial Government for approval. The total annual budget, originally set at 50,000 yuan, has been increased by 7,000 yuan, totaling 57,000 yuan. The internal organization is divided into four sections to manage the office affairs. The first section: Secretary Guan Gengze, clerks Li Fengli, Ge Tianmin, and Jin Zhenduo; the second section: Secretary Shen Zutong, clerks Lin Heng, Li Hongtu, and Li Chunqi; the third section: Secretary Cao Chengzong, clerks Huang Jiashi, Yu Lianying, and Xia Zhongqi; the fourth section: Secretary Luo Zhongwen, clerks Wang Yuxiang, Chang Enji, Tong Guoxiang, and Chen Guangshan. The office regulations are listed below: (Article 1) This Commissioner shall, in accordance with the regulations set by the Ministry, comprehensively manage foreign affairs in this province. (Article 2) This Commissioner's Office shall be called the Foreign Ministry's Liaoning Foreign Affairs Commissioner's Office. (Article 3) The Office shall have the following sections: 1. First Section, 2. Second Section, 3. Third Section. (Article 4) The First Section shall manage the Office's accounting, general affairs, safekeeping of documents, guarding of seals, receiving and dispatching of communications, and matters not belonging to other sections. (Article 5) The Second Section shall be responsible for drafting and translating documents to and from Western countries, as well as matters related to dealings and interactions with those countries. (Article 6) The Third Section shall be responsible for drafting and translating documents to and from Japan, as well as matters related to dealings and interactions with that country. (Article 7) The Fourth Section shall be responsible for drafting and translating documents to and from Russia, as well as matters related to dealings and interactions with that country, and managing Russian expatriate affairs. (Article 8) The Office shall have six secretaries, with two secretaries responsible for drafting confidential documents and four secretaries responsible for the affairs of each section. (Article 9) Each section shall have several clerks, the number to be determined based on the complexity of the affairs. (Article 10) For drafting, recording, and compilation purposes, each section may employ clerks, the number to be determined based on the complexity of the affairs. (Article 11) Secretaries, under the direction of the Commissioner, shall be in charge of the affairs of a section and shall have the responsibility of supervising the personnel in their section. (Article 12) Clerks and employees shall, in consultation with the secretaries, be responsible for the affairs of each section. (Article 13) If there are any changes to these regulations, they may be revised at any time. (Article 14) These regulations shall take effect from the date of approval. (April 23rd)

Important News Two

Closure of the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine

Harbin Dispatch: The Zhalainuoer Coal Mine is one of the three major coal mines in Northern Manchuria. Although its coal is not as heavy and long-burning as that of Muling, or as powerfully heating as that of Hegang, its sixteen coal pits produce forty to fifty trainloads per day, supplying the Eastern Railway, making it a major source. Last year, Zhalainuoer was captured by the Russian army, who immediately carried out destruction, damaging all the coal pit water pipes and oil-drawing machines. The pits were flooded with several feet of water. After the war, efforts were made to restore it, but only the ninth pit could be excavated as normal, producing only one or two trainloads per day. The others could not be restored. The Eastern Railway authorities, considering the mine unable to operate, switched to purchasing coal from Suicheng in Russia as a substitute. All the miners and staff of the mine were paid off and dismissed at the beginning of this month. The Zhalainuoer Coal Mine, which had been in operation for many years, is unlikely to be reopened. It is rumored that the Russian intention is that with the closure of the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine, Hegang, being far away in the Lower Jiang Tangyuan, is inconvenient for transportation, and Muling's production is small, producing only a dozen or so trainloads per day. If something were to happen, the supply of Russian Suicheng coal would be cut off, the Eastern Railway would feel a lack of fuel, and there would be a danger of trains stopping and transportation being disrupted, allowing the Russian side to do as they please. Therefore, the closure of the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine is very disadvantageous to our side.

Local Communications

Songjiang

Sijing Town Robbed for the Second Time: Sijing Town in this county is a prosperous commercial center. Since being robbed by bandits once before two years ago, local figures have felt that the local defense capabilities are weak and have been organizing a defense corps. Recently, with the bandit robberies in Zhangyan and other places, Sijing has implemented strict precautions. However, today (the 28th), when the Litong steamer traveling from Songjiang to Sijing was passing through Tangqiao, someone from Sijing suddenly claimed that there were more than 200 bandits in the town at about 2:00 PM, led by someone carrying a large white-bordered red flag. The police officers of the town's Public Security Bureau and the defense corps came out to resist, fearing that they would be outnumbered and unable to avoid being robbed. The passengers on the boat dared not continue and returned to Songjiang. The county government also received a long-distance phone call from Xinzhuang, from those who had escaped from Sijing, reporting the bandit situation and requesting the dispatch of troops for rescue. Soon after, a messenger from Sijing arrived in Songjiang and reported to the County Public Security Bureau. County Magistrate Jin, after receiving the report, immediately dispatched two platoons of the county police and consulted with the 3rd Battalion of the 2nd Regiment of the Artillery Training Corps of the Central Military Academy stationed in Songjiang to send troops to travel with the police force on the Litong steamer to Sijing to block and suppress the bandits. Li Wenlai, the owner of a certain rice shop in Sijing, happened to be in Songjiang for business. His family sent someone to Songjiang to urge him to return to Sijing. It is heard that the bandits came from Qingpu and landed on the west side of the town and swarmed into the town, robbing all the way to Zhangjing Bridge for four hours. However, there is no confirmed information about the robbery. The water police, after hearing the news, also mobilized warships and rushed to suppress the bandits.

Suzhou

Lu Genrong Applies to Terminate Imprisonment, Application Denied: Lu Genrong, involved in the master-servant love affair case, was sentenced to two years in prison after the third trial last year. Lu remained dissatisfied and filed an extraordinary appeal. The case has not yet been remanded. Recently, Lu, suffering from illness while in custody, applied for termination of imprisonment. The High Court sent officials to investigate the prison and yesterday (the 28th) issued a ruling rejecting Lu Genrong's application for termination of imprisonment.

Dongzhu Hostage Escapes the Same Night: Dongzhu Town in Guangfu Township, in this county, was raided by more than 50 bandits at about 9 PM on the night before last (the 26th). Ge Wenzhi (yesterday mistakenly reported as Guo Ziren), a shop assistant at Renchang Nanhua Store, was kidnapped. They fled towards the South Taihu Lake. The bandits demanded 20,000 yuan from Ge, ordering him to notify his family to prepare the money for his release. Ge Wenzhi repeatedly pleaded with the bandits, saying that he had no property and would rather die than pay the money. At that time, another bandit interjected and they drove to Sanyang, releasing Ge ashore. Ge has now safely returned home.

Extortionist Policemen Handed Over to the District Court: Yu Jinzhou and Chen Shouzhang, two policemen from the Water Patrol Team of the County Public Security Bureau, were caught by Director Min of the Tuantuan District Office on the 25th for extorting a large sum of money from soil vendor Wang Waitou. Director Cao Ping of the Bureau personally brought them to the bureau for investigation. Director Cao, feeling that the reputation of the entire bureau had been completely tarnished by the extortion case of his subordinates, handed over the two offenders, Yu and Chen, to the District Court for handling yesterday (the 28th). The case also involves Wu Shaowu, the captain of the Second Squadron of the County Police. Director Cao has dispatched inspectors to investigate thoroughly.

Verdict in the Li-Cheng Mutual Lawsuit: In the case of mutual lawsuits between former Premier Li Genyuan and his abandoned concubine Cheng Peiyi, the Wuxian District Court pronounced its verdict at 2 PM yesterday. The main points are as follows: In Li Genyuan's suit against Cheng Peiyi et al. for defamation and fraud, and Cheng Peiyi's counterclaim, Cheng Peiyi is found guilty of slander and fined 15 yuan. If the fine is not paid, one yuan will be deducted for each day of imprisonment. Cheng Peiyi, Li Genyuan, Ma Shulan, Shi Rushi, and Cheng Peiyi are acquitted of the remaining charges.

Bandit Woman in Qionglong Mountain Robbery Sent to Headquarters: The Zhenguan Taoist Temple on Qionglong Mountain in Shanquanqiao, Mudu Township in this county, was robbed by five bandits and four people were shot a few days ago. It was later learned that the perpetrators were the former guard team member Lao Pan et al. from Shanquanqiao. When the guard team went to arrest them, Pan fled and was shot and killed by the guard team. Pan's mistress, Han, was captured and a lot of stolen goods were found. She was transferred to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation. Because the case involved banditry, she was sent to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters for interrogation yesterday morning.

Jiading

Woman Found to Have Been Kidnapped: Last night (the 26th) at 9 PM, the Anting Defense Corps checked passengers at the Xinxin Hotel in Dongjie and found a young woman with crystal-rimmed glasses and leather shoes to be suspicious. When questioned, she replied that her mother's family name was Wang, she was 22 years old from Pinghu, and she was married to Shen Wusheng, a tailor from the same town, and lived in Shanghai's Jiangyuan Lane. Three years ago, Wusheng abandoned his profession to join the army and has not been heard from since. On the 21st, she met Wang, a shop assistant at a dowry shop, who lured her to visit her hometown, and sent the purchased clothing materials worth 17 yuan to a friend. They took the train to this place and stayed at the Lu family's house in Lujiacun for three nights. On the fourth day, the Lu couple searched her for the 18 yuan she had with her and forced her to marry someone with a certain surname. Because she refused, she was tied with ropes. She shouted for help and escaped to stay at the inn. The Defense Corps, considering the case involved kidnapping, asked the 8th District Office for instructions. District Chief Qian, finding that Lujiacun was under the jurisdiction of another district, refused to accept the case and ordered the suspect to report to the jurisdictional agency.

Change of District Chief in the Third District: The County Government previously received an order from the Provincial Government to transfer Wu Xishou, the chief of the Third District, to the Fifth District, and to appoint Lu Jing to fill the vacant position, causing the heads of various townships in the Third District to jointly petition to retain Wu and reject Lu, causing an uproar. Now, a citizen surnamed Yang from the Third District sent a letter to the new District Chief Lu Jing, exposing the underlying cause of the uproar. Then, a clerk surnamed Xu from the district office met with Lu and proposed conditions, saying that if he did not transfer the clerks in the office, he could guarantee safety. It is heard that District Chief Lu immediately agreed and asked him to pass on the message, and it was decided that he would take office on May 1st.

Completion of Rebuilding of the East Suspension Bridge: The suspension bridge outside the East Gate had been in disrepair for many years, making it inconvenient for vehicles to travel. Recently, with the opening of the Jialuo Motor Road, the number of vehicles increased, so the authorities allocated funds to rebuild the iron-and-cement bridge, which began construction last month and has now been completed, making it convenient for travelers.

Fengxian

Methods Agreed Upon for Price Stabilization: The first phase of price stabilization is currently in the process of creating registers and distributing tickets. All the methods have also been agreed upon. It is estimated that there are more than 30,400 poor households in the county, with a total of more than 77,220 people, who are all entitled to four jin of rice per household. Calculated at a fixed price of 160 cash per jin, each household should pay 640 cash, with more added proportionally.

County Administrative Conference: The minutes of the second County Administrative Conference of this session have been printed and distributed. The conference lasted four days, with 38 members attending, and a total of 57 cases were discussed and decided. Among the important ones from the finance group are the county's land tax for the 19th year, which will be based on the 5% surcharge collected in the 18th year. The expenses for May and June of the 18th year will be issued at 80% for the time being. If they have already been reduced to 80%, they will remain unchanged. Among the important ones from the political affairs group are the spring relief and the second phase of price stabilization. The County Government Secretariat has already sent the resolutions to the Provincial Government separately and has also sent them to various agencies for their reference.

Inspection After the Robbery of the Han Family: The Han Yikang family in the South 3 Li of Zhuanghang was robbed of clothing and bedding on the 24th. It was raining at the time. By the time the Second Squad of the County Police arrived, it was too late. Now, Wang Jinchuan, the captain of the Water Public Security Squad, went to inspect the scene today together with Squad Captain Yang.

Wuxi

A Succession of Robberies: The night-shift ferry boat traveling between this county and Zhouzhuang in Jiangyin County was attacked by a bandit boat while traveling from Wuxi to Zhouzhuang at Hujia Duhan, Tianshang City, the day before yesterday. Nine bandits on the boat, each holding a pistol and flashlight, jumped onto the ferry boat and forced the boat owner, Zhou Aji, to hand over the goods and money, and stripped the clothes of all the passengers, looting at will. After about half an hour, they carried the stolen goods back to their original boat and fled. After counting, the boat owner and passengers lost about 400 yuan in total. Also, the home of Yan Cheng根, a farmer in Zhang Ming Bridge, Wanan City, was visited by more than ten bandits at about 4 AM on the night of that day. They broke down the door and ransacked the house, robbing them of more than 100 yuan in cash and more than a dozen pieces of clothing, for a total loss of more than 200 yuan. Also, yesterday evening, Qian Tongzhi, the educational commissioner of the Mao學匕 School District in Yangming Township, received 370 yuan in funding for the schools for April at the Education Bureau. On his way back to his hometown from the city, he was attacked by five bandits near Dongfeng. They produced weapons and threatened him in every way, eventually robbing him of the 370 yuan he had received. Afterward, Qian reported to Director Lu of the Education Bureau, who forwarded the report to Director Huang of the Public Security Bureau, ordering them to investigate.

Buddhist Monk Extortionist Arrested and Sent to the Bureau: Yang Xu (also known as Yang Pan根) and Gao Xingquan, two local ruffians from the Yuhuang Temple on Furong Mountain in the Sixth District (Bashiqiao), carrying fake pistols, went to the top of the mountain and forced their way into the monastery at midnight the day before yesterday. They broke into the meditation room and threatened the abbot with fake pistols, claiming that they wanted to borrow 500 yuan, or they would take his life. As a result, the abbot gave them 70 yuan and they left. Afterward, the members of the Bashiqiao Defense Corps arrested Gao Xingquan, a person involved in the case, and detained him at the corps headquarters. Yesterday, Xue Furui, the captain of the Detective Squad of the County Public Security Bureau, also received a secret report and immediately ordered squad members Dai Shouquan et al. to arrest Yang Xu and bring him to the bureau. Qian, the Chief of the Judicial Section, interrogated him and Yang confessed to extorting 70 yuan with a fake pistol and spending it. He was immediately ordered to be detained pending interrogation by the county.

Progress Report on the Wuxi-Changzhou Provincial Road: Since the start of construction of the Wuxi-Changzhou Provincial Road, the County Government and the Construction Bureau have been actively proceeding, but at this time of year when farmers are busy with farming and silkworm raising, they are all concerned about their livelihoods and cannot respond to the conscription. The villagers of the Eighth and Ninth Districts of this county publicly elected Chen Taihuan, Zhu Meiji, Huang Junyu, and six others as representatives to go to the Construction Department in the Provincial Government to petition for a postponement, carrying a public petition. Secretary-General Zhang came forward to receive them, and the representatives presented their petition. Secretary-General Zhang expressed his acceptance and promised to postpone the construction until after autumn. The representatives returned to Wuxi yesterday. Also, in order to urge the progress, County Magistrate Sun has ordered the detention of Liang Shu Dan Zixiang, Chen Jinhe, and Zhang Meichu, who neglected road duties, to serve as a warning to others.

Changzhou

Liu Lei Appointed Director of the Public Security Bureau: Li Leng, Director of the Wuyi Public Security Bureau, was appointed County Magistrate of Jiangyin and went to the province the day before yesterday to report on his mission, including the investigation into the Red Pill organization. He returned to Changzhou on the 26th. It is heard that Liu Lei has been appointed as the director of the Wuyi Public Security Bureau and is scheduled to come to Changzhou on the 30th to take over on May 1st. It is said that the captured witnesses from the Red Pill organization will be transferred to the judiciary for handling.

District Chiefs Again Petition for the Abolition of Tax Collection Officers: The dispute between the District Chiefs and the tax collection officers in Wuyi has been going on for a long time. Former County Magistrate Zhu ordered the Finance Bureau to abolish the tax collection officers, and the responsibility for tax collection was to be handled by the District, Township, and Village Offices. The Finance Bureau has submitted a request to the Finance Department for approval. Recently, the District Chiefs jointly submitted a petition to County Magistrate Wu, requesting him to forward it to the Finance Department and to order the Finance Bureau to abolish the tax collection officers as soon as possible.

Chamber of Commerce Promotes Straw Hat Industry: The Wuyi Chamber of Commerce, seeing the prosperity of the straw hat industry in Yuyao County, Zhejiang, where there is little unemployment, sent a special agent, Shi Zhongxuan, to investigate. After returning to Changzhou and reporting, they requested the county to send one male and one female worker to Changzhou on the 27th to test the work in the Chamber of Commerce. Seeing that they were very quick and agile in their production and that the woven straw hats were very fine, they decided to recruit 20 female workers to be taught at the Poor Children's Home. They will graduate in about a month and then teach each other, which will be easy to promote. It is also heard that each person earns 20-30 yuan per month.

Prosecutors Inspect Theft Case: Qian Huolin, a thief who robbed the Ma Jinchun family in the area under the jurisdiction of the Fifth Outpost of the First Branch of the Longhu Public Security Bureau of Wuyi, was handed over to the County Court for trial. At the trial, the victim stated that he saw Qian Huolin inside the house during the robbery. The prosecutor, considering the importance of the case, led the police on the 27th to inspect the scene of the robbery to verify the facts.

Nantong

Banditry Breaks Out Again, Telegram Requesting the Hu Battalion to Return to Defend: The Fifth Division Hu Battalion, sent by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to Nantong to suppress bandits, has opened the way to Haimen, and the bandit forces have become resurgent. Local circles have sent representatives to Shanghai to petition for a temporary exemption from transfer. Commander Xiong telegraphed his approval to temporarily station them there. On the 27th, the County Government telegraphed Hu Battalion Commander Haimen, saying that because the esteemed battalion had temporarily opened the way to Haimen to inspect the forces, the bandits took the opportunity to act. Alarms have been frequent in recent days, and there is a sense of imminent crisis. The city and the countryside are shaking together, and people are extremely fearful. Due to the previous electricity, the esteemed battalion leader, please consider the urgency of the local situation, and return to the original defense. Battalion Commander Hu immediately telegraphed a reply, stating that he would leave Haimen on the 29th and return to Tongcheng.

Petitioning to Seal Up the Property of a Corrupt Police Captain: Former County Police Captain Yan Diannan was corrupt and unlawful during his tenure, and looted underlings in Yudong, Pingchao, and other districts, and transported the stolen goods to the city openly. The provincial order to dismiss him was issued, and Yan fled to Shanghai in fear of punishment. Now, representatives of local agencies, considering that Yan is from Nantong and has a family living in Tongcheng, have specially presented a petition to the province, requesting the County Government to first seal up Yan Diannan's property and then issue an arrest warrant to bring him to justice.

Jiangyin

Dispatching Commissioners to Investigate Banditry: The Songhu Garrison Headquarters, to investigate bandit activity in various counties, dispatches personnel to inspect each county monthly. The day before yesterday, it commissioned Lieutenant Colonel Aide-de-Camp Jin Yuxi to come to Cheng (Jiangyin) to investigate, and he went to the county government for liaison. Aide-de-Camp Jin is scheduled to go to Nanjing on the 27th.

Robbery Occurs in Binjiang Township: At midnight on the 26th, the home of Zhou Genlang, a villager in Shuyuan Village, Binjiang Township, north of the city, was broken into by more than ten robbers. The perpetrators burned Zhou Genlang with fire, robbed him of cloth and silver dollars, and then broke through the wall to the home of Zhou Jichuan in the Zou family, where they ransacked before leaving.

Female Worker Commits Suicide After Being Dismissed for Taking Arsenic: The wife of Yang Silang of Chenjia Village, north of the city gate, worked in the spinning room of the Liyong Yarn Factory. The day before yesterday, a cotton inspector found a small amount of cotton in the sole of her shoe and reported it to the accounting office, which immediately dismissed her. After Yang Silang's wife returned home, she took red arsenic and died. The Workers' Association believes that the Liyong accounting office is too harsh and intends to appeal on her behalf to demonstrate humanity.

Jingjiang

Traveler Kidnapped on the Way: Jingjiang City and Huangqiao in Taixing have two fast boats that travel back and forth once a day. On the 25th, a fast boat from Huangqiao was carrying passengers when, about ten miles from the city at Changdai Market, bandits suddenly appeared with pistols and ordered the boat to stop. They kidnapped a Huangqiao merchant. Village Head Shot Dead by Bandits: At the second watch (around 10 PM) on the 24th, Tang Shouqing, the village head of the 23rd Tu (unit of local administration) in the eastern part of the Third District, was urgently knocked on his door by someone speaking with a local accent who claimed to have an important document from the county government. Tang Shouqing hurriedly opened the door, and the robbers rushed in, seized Shouqing, and shot him. The first shot hit his throat, and the second hit the back of his head, exiting through his nose. He died instantly. As the robbers left, they left a note for his wife, the contents of which were absurd.

Large Number of Suspects Arrested: The Chang'an City Security Corps, together with the guerrilla队, arrested Xia Xincai, Zhang Yaolang, Chang Guangsheng, Wang Zizhong, Xia Zhengfang, Liu Sankun, Ji Qiaolin, Wang Rusong, Lu Yingen, Xia Baozong, Ji Songlin, Xia Zhengming, Chang Fusheng, Chen Yusheng, Xia Zhengshu, and Wang Baosheng, a total of sixteen people, at the Wenwu Temple on the 25th. On the 26th, they were transferred to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Rugao

Bandits Set Fire to Two Homes: The home of Ji Shaochuan, the head of Hedong Township in Rugao City, was attacked by over a hundred bandits at around 12 AM on the 24th. They carried firearms, electric lights, and incendiary materials and set fire to the house. In an instant, more than twenty rooms were reduced to ashes. At the same time, the home of Ji Shaoqing in Shaojiazhuang, Yelin Township, was also set on fire by bandits, burning over fifty thatched and tiled rooms. The total loss for both families is estimated at 1.22 million yuan.

Large Quantity of Barley Seized at Zhanghuang Port: The second branch station and the water police team of Zhanghuang Port seized over five hundred dan (approximately 50,000 kg) of illegally transported barley on the 30th, loaded on ten boats. The goods were immediately impounded, and it has now been decided to sell it at a fair price.

Yangzhou

Walking Group Sets Departure Date from Yangzhou: Xie Fensheng and other members of the National Walking Group arrived at the Luyang Hostel in Yangzhou via Dudu River, Liuhe, Yizheng, and Shierxu. They visited various institutions in recent days. On the 26th and 27th, the entire group toured scenic spots such as Tianning Temple and Slender West Lake, taking pictures everywhere to document their journey. They are scheduled to head north along the canal on the 29th.

Primary Schools to Resume Classes on a Set Date: Primary schools in the city and suburbs had been on strike for several days due to unpaid salaries. The county has now raised enough funds for half a month's salaries and distributed them to the Education Bureau. The schools were distributed at the afternoon of the 27th and are scheduled to resume classes on the 28th.

Gaoyou

Fan Pawnshop Robbery Solved: The Hengxing Pawnshop in Fanchuan Town, under the jurisdiction of the county, was robbed the night before last, resulting in a significant loss of jewelry. Chen, the nephew of the pawnshop manager, and Sha, a carpenter working at the pawnshop, were lodging in the pawnshop at the time. Chen made an excuse to go home the next morning, which aroused the suspicion of the pawnshop staff. In the past two days, the actions of the carpenter Sha have also been quite suspicious. They were beaten and interrogated for a long time, and they finally confessed that they had only received three jin ten liang (about 1.85 kg) of pure gold jewelry, and the rest was taken away by Chen. Sha's stolen goods have been completely handed over, but Chen has already fled and cannot be recovered. The manager of the pawnshop sent a telegram to the owner of the pawnshop in Zhenjiang yesterday to request instructions.

Taizhou

Organizing a Home Guard: Due to the rampant banditry in the villages west of Linhai, especially in Huangshadianxi, local people have jointly discussed the matter and decided to add forty members to the home guard to defend themselves. The expenses will be borne by the local community and should be implemented soon.

Troops Dispatched to Suppress Clan Fighting: The Huang, Sha, Gao, and Xie clans in the villages west of Linhai have recently started a conflict over a minor matter. Both sides gathered and engaged in clan fighting, injuring many people. Jiang Zhiying, the battalion commander of the First Battalion of the Third Regiment of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team stationed in the city, learned of the matter and dispatched two companies of troops to suppress the fighting yesterday (the 24th).

Jiaxing

Chief of Public Security Sub-bureau Arrested: Wu Ming, the chief of the Wangjiangjing Public Security Sub-bureau in Jiaxing, has not been properly managing police affairs, and local people have many complaints. Recently, he has been imposing fines arbitrarily for various cases without issuing receipts. Local people have now listed the charges and filed a complaint with the province. After an investigation, the province ordered the county government to instruct the County Public Security Bureau to arrest Wu and place him under custody at the County Public Security Bureau. Yesterday, the case was sent to the local branch court for legal investigation. After the prosecutor opened the court for interrogation, Wu Ming was returned to the County Public Security Bureau for custody.

Rice Prices Increase Again: The price of rice in Jiaxing has gradually increased to sixteen yuan per shi (approximately 94 kg). The Rice Price Evaluation Committee tried to limit it, temporarily setting the price at sixteen yuan to maintain people's livelihood. However, at the sixteenth Rice Price Evaluation Committee meeting the day before yesterday, rice merchant representative Gao Yingjing reported that the wholesale price of winter rice was sixteen yuan eight jiao five fen (1.685 yuan) and that they were unwilling to sell it at that price. Therefore, they requested a price increase. After repeated discussions, the meeting decided to order rice merchants to temporarily maintain the original price until May 3rd. It was stipulated that winter rice, white rice, and pointed rice would each be priced at sixteen yuan per shi, and foreign rice would be priced at fifteen yuan five jiao per shi, with no deviations allowed. However, soon after the decision was made, some rice merchants, such as so and so, verbally notified their colleagues on the morning of the 28th that they would increase the price of rice by four jiao per shi without authorization. As a result, the rice price set by this committee was ineffective.

Jiashan

County Government Raises Construction Bonds: The County Government, following an order from the Provincial Department of Construction, is raising 180,000 yuan in construction bonds. County Magistrate Shen first sent a letter to agencies, organizations, gentry, and merchants to organize a Construction Bond Raising Committee, which will then hold regular meetings to solicit donations.

New Silkworm Seed Farm Established in the City: Jiashan has never produced its own silkworm seeds. They have either come from local species from Xinchang and Shengxian or have been sold by merchants from Yuhang. The quality of the silkworm season depends entirely on the quality of the silkworm seeds. Recently, silkworm industry experts Ms. Wu Renzhao and Ms. Yao Shumen have invested in and organized the Jiashan Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Farm in the south of the city with over twenty years of experience in the silkworm industry. They will personally supervise, cultivate, and select improved cocoon seeds from excellent original seeds that are praised by silk mills for their rich silk content and strong silkworms, and sell them to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other regions. Many people have heard of them and are making reservations daily. It is said that the price of cocoons raised from these improved seeds is much higher than that of ordinary cocoons.

Xiaoshan

County Magistrate Du Accused of Malfeasance: County Magistrate Du Shihua of Xiaoshan previously arrested Shen Zengfeng, a member of the Eastern Township Changxiang Village, and detained him for several days without interrogation. He did not obtain permission from the local senior Party department beforehand. The First Branch of the Second District telegraphed the County Party Department to handle the matter, claiming that the County Government had violated Party discipline. The County Party Department investigated and confirmed that the Party member had not committed any legally criminal acts and sent a letter to the county government to release him. Recently, Shen Zengfeng has accused County Magistrate Du Shihua of acting illegally and derelicting his duty, claiming that human rights are not protected, and has filed a lawsuit with the County Court, requesting Prosecutor Yang to file a public prosecution based on the two crimes of malfeasance and abuse of arrest. After receiving the complaint, the Prosecutor's Office summoned both parties for a court hearing at 1 PM on the 25th.

District Offices Scheduled to Be Established on May 1st: The district offices of Xiaoshan County have been officially established on May 1st. County Magistrate Du has appointed the six district chiefs: Xu Yuanzhang, chief of the First District; Huang Zuluo, chief of the Second District; Wang Jie, chief of the Third District; Ge Shiyou, chief of the Fourth District; Zhu Zhiyang, chief of the Fifth District; and Yu Bin, chief of the Sixth District. The existing self-government instructors are required to transfer all unfinished work to the district offices for takeover before the 30th of this month.

Poor Silkworm Harvest in Dongzou: Farmers in the Nansha area of Dongxiang, Xiaoshan, mainly rely on sericulture as a sideline occupation. This year, the local Silk Cocoon Cooperative purchased Japanese silkworm seeds from Shanghai and distributed them to farmers for cultivation, totaling more than 3,000 sheets. However, the weather after Guyu (around April 20) was abnormal, with alternating periods of extreme cold and sultry heat, and frequent thunderstorms. Many young silkworms died, so the harvest will inevitably be greatly reduced.

Shangyu

Prelude to Park Construction: Parks are one of the components of material construction, and now various counties are successively constructing them. Wuyu (Shangyu) is still lacking. Recently, residents Qian Youlan and Liu Hao, etc., proposed the matter to the administrative meeting, which resolved to forward it to the County Construction Committee for implementation. Wang Jilao sent a letter to Fan Yunshu, agreeing to purchase more than ten mu of land outside the southern suburbs that he owned as the foundation for the park. The construction funds will be allocated from the construction funds of the Mass Education Center by Director of Education Che Mingluan in consultation with the Preparatory Committee of the Mass Education Center, which has been allocated two thousand yuan. It was heard yesterday that the Construction Committee is planning to hold a meeting to discuss the project plan.

Clarifying Misunderstandings About the Suspension of Land Reporting: The County Government previously received a telegram from the Provincial Department ordering that land reporting be completed by the end of April. For a time, there were rumors among the people that those who had already handled it had stopped, and those who had not handled it had slowed down. County Magistrate Zhang Jingxu went to the Provincial Civil Affairs Department on the 13th to inquire about the meaning of the so-called "deadline of the end of April," which was for the purpose of reviewing the reporting work over the past year and determining follow-up methods. Moreover, this matter is of great importance to the livelihood of the people, and it is not appropriate to abandon it halfway. A notice was issued to the public on the 25th.

Bandit Suspect Temporarily Released on Bail: On the evening of the 14th, the home of He Caizhao in Shan'ao, Dongxiang, was robbed by bandits. The day after the incident, a suspect named Ye Liangen was apprehended. At the same time, Judge Zhu Yao came to inspect the scene and found a bandit's umbrella engraved with the name "Fu Chai Defu, Mojiashu Village, Shangyu-Xinchang border." An investigation was launched, and it was confirmed that such a person existed. The county defense team stationed in the city, together with the security team, rushed to the village and escorted him to the county government for interrogation. He claimed that he was a farmer with four brothers, one of whom was teaching at the nearby Houtou Elementary School. His brother took the umbrella to the school, which was robbed last year. It was raining at the time, and the bandits took the umbrella along with them. He did not expect that this would lead to trouble. An order was issued for his detention. His family, hearing the news, sought help everywhere. On the afternoon of the 26th, Xu Guoren from the Civilian Factory temporarily released him on bail.

Shaoxing

Continued Interrogation in the Fengqiao Riot Case: A riot occurred in Fengqiao Town, Zhuji, on the 25th. It is now reported that there were sixty or seventy bandits involved that day. They first cut the telephone lines and went to the anti-smuggling camp, where they robbed three guns. They then went to the public security sub-bureau, searched and robbed firearms, and beat policemen Chen Xiang and Luo Cheng to death. Then, they went to the market and destroyed and robbed the Jiahe and Chen Songmao rice shops and went to the Hengda General Merchandise Store, taking away a large number of straw hats. Afterwards, more than thirty bandits had lunch near the Ginkgo tree and left in the direction of Ruanjiabu. According to the County Detective's report, the bandits in Fengqiao have not completely retreated, and there are slogans in Dagouxi Village above Xiejiaqiao calling for the overthrow of the village committee and the land reporting office.

Extortion Case Involving Rice Merchants in City and Countryside: Rice prices in Shaoxing have been soaring repeatedly due to a lack of supply and poor harvests, causing extreme hardship for the people. Recently, rice merchants in the city and countryside, such as Zhao Wanchun in Kezhen, Song Jitai outside Wuyunmen, and Sanyu Xintaiyuan and other rice shops in the urban area, have received anonymous threatening letters demanding that they set fair prices within a limited time or face destruction. The matter has been referred by the County Chamber of Commerce to the County Government for investigation. Due to the connection with people's food and public security, County Magistrate Tang has issued a notice promising to find ways to provide relief.

The Strength of the Philippines in the Far Eastern Games

Officials and Athletes... All Decided

Early May... Departing for Japan

Basketball and Volleyball are the Strongest, Will Face China in the Finals. Track and Field Long-Distance Running is Not as Good as Japan, Soccer Can Win the Runner-up. Whether or Not the Championship Can Be Obtained Depends Entirely on Swimming and Baseball. Swimming Has a Strong Japanese Enemy, and Chinese Baseball is Also Formidable (Manila Correspondence). Since the last Far Eastern Games in Shanghai, the Philippines have been very enthusiastic and determined to avenge their defeat in this year's games in order to win the Far Eastern hegemony and capture the Emperor's Cup, to promote the bravery of athletes from the equatorial country. This year, the Philippine Islands began preparations for the Games the earliest, starting with local preliminaries in January. In February, a carnival was held in Manila, bringing together the best athletes in the country. The results were amazing, and new records were frequently set. The Philippine Islands will send a total of more than 160 athletes and other personnel to Japan, led by Deputy Secretary of Agriculture George. They will arrive in Yokohama in early May. All schools in the Philippines are now on vacation. Due to the local climate, the summer vacation is from March to June every year. Taking advantage of this great opportunity, various sports are being carried out enthusiastically. All the Philippine athletes are living together in the training center in Manila, and specialists are directing their training every day. The various competition committees of the Philippine Islands are as follows:

(1) List of All Staff Members

(Head of the delegation) Deputy Secretary of Agriculture Mr. George, Mr. Bitchi, Dr. Rippino

(Track and Field Committee) Mr. Silafan, Mr. Fuqulu Lunate, (Former Philippine University Sprinter) Mr. Nicodti, Mr. Niu Man (U.S. Army)

(Swimming Committee) Mr. Gadi, (Philippine University) Mr. Hewaqi (Youth Association)

(Baseball Committee) Mr. Fulan, (Philippine University) Mr. Mariano

(Tennis Committee) Dr. Bigutuo Lu

(Basketball Committee) Mr. Birdo

(Volleyball Committee) Mr. Bablu, Ms. Carmen

(Soccer Committee) Mr. Tidyuqiu Mixin

(2) Strength of Various Competitions

According to a conversation with Dr. Ilanan, President of the Philippine Athletic Association (P.A.A.F.), the Philippine athletes in the non-official boxing event that has been added this year will probably have no opponents. In official competitions, Japan has the most hope in track and field and tennis. China is confident in soccer. The Philippines is the strongest in basketball and volleyball. Therefore, whether or not the Philippines can win the championship this time depends entirely on swimming and baseball. Unfortunately, there has been a dispute among the Philippine swimming athletes, and baseball is gradually declining. At the last Far Eastern Games, the Philippine baseball team was completely wiped out. Last year, the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun baseball team defeated the entire Philippine Islands in an expedition. Dr. Ilanan also said that even Japan is not optimistic about this year's games and will inevitably have a tough fight with the emerging China. According to reliable sources, the strengths of the Philippine athletes in various competitions are as follows:

(3) Track and Field Short-Distance Running Has Surprising Performances

The Philippines has always been known for its short and medium distances, with the most outstanding athletes. Because long-distance running is not as good as Japan, it has recently lost many track and field championships. Its short-distance running often has surprising performances. For example, Mr. Shenzhaga's 100-meter time, with the wind, is 10.4 seconds, equalling the world record. Other athletes in hurdles, high jump, and high hurdles are also admirable. Its various track and field results are as follows:

(4) Unreliable Swimming Athletes

Since the 6th Osaka Games to the 8th Shanghai Games, the Philippines have won swimming championships as easily as picking things out of a bag. Therefore, the Philippine Islands are quite proud of swimming competitions. However, the unfavorable aspect of this year's Games for the Philippines is that the Games are in May, and the climate of Japan and the Philippines is very different. Philippine athletes are mostly afraid of the cold, which may prevent them from defeating Japan. This year, nine outstanding Philippine athletes have withdrawn from the delegation due to unfair judging during the preliminaries and cannot participate in the Games. Japanese outstanding athletes will never go to other countries to compete before the Far Eastern Games open. This may prevent the Philippines from defeating Japan again. According to general speculation, Japan has a 60% chance of winning the swimming championship this year, and the Philippines only has 40%. The Philippine athletes' records in various events are as follows:

(50 meters) Mr. Wuerjia, Mr. Ali (Each 57.5 seconds), Mr. Shanweng Gusi Zhi (58 seconds), Mr. Haijialiya (58.5 seconds)

The above records are all from competitions in 25-meter swimming pools.

(6) It May Be Difficult to Win the Tennis Championship

Philippine tennis has won several championships in the history of the Far Eastern Games, but it has recently declined and has been repeatedly suppressed by the Chinese and Japanese armies. At this year's Carnival, China defeated the Philippine athletes, and Japan defeated the Chinese athletes again. The best athletes in the Philippine Islands are the Arasin brothers. Due to their professional relationship, it is difficult to predict whether they will be able to participate. In future Games, it may be difficult for the Philippine Islands to win the championship. In this year's basketball game, China and the Philippines will inevitably have a fierce and bloody battle. Next Year's National Games Scheduled for April

Preparatory Committee Sets the Games for April 15th to 24th

National Government Orders Ministry of Finance to Allocate 100,000 Yuan Immediately for Construction

This newspaper, 28th Nanjing dispatch: The National Government instructed the Ministry of Finance that according to the report submitted by Lin Sen and others of the National Games Preparatory Committee, they were ordered to prepare for next year's National Games, and have already held the first preparatory committee meeting, planning to set the meeting date from April 15th to April 24th of the 20th year [of the Republic]. Please order the Ministry of Finance to allocate 100,000 yuan as the first installment of the 500,000 yuan of approved expenses, so that urgent and important construction projects can be started immediately. As for the remaining 400,000 yuan, please also designate funds to be allocated in installments, etc., and instruct them to act accordingly.

Jiangsu-Zhejiang Middle School Sports Meet

Starts Today

The joint sports meet of ten middle schools in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces is scheduled to be held in Suzhou on the 29th and 30th of this month. Each team has successively arrived and is being hosted separately by four schools, including Suzhou Cuiying. Nanjing Jinling Middle School Affiliated and Jiaxing Xiuzhou Middle School have declared their withdrawal. Therefore, only nine schools are participating in the competition this time. The order of competition has been detailed in previous reports. However, due to curriculum schedules, track and field events must be held at 3:00 PM. Ball games will still be held in the morning.

Shandong Middle School Sports Meet

Grand Opening Ceremony

(Jinan Correspondence) The long-prepared First Shandong Provincial Middle School Spring Joint Sports Meet opened at 8:00 AM on the 25th at the People's Sports Field outside Nanweimen. Participating were athletes from various schools, representatives from various organizations, and spectators from all walks of life, totaling over 30,000 people. Details are recorded below:

Venue Arrangement: The main gate is in the northwest corner, constructed with a high pine archway, intertwined with Party flags and national flags, bearing the words "First Shandong Provincial Middle School Spring Joint Sports Meet". Inside the gate is the registration area. The command platform is located in the center of the field, with a portrait of the late Premier hanging above the central eastern side of the chairman's stand. Below are the prizes. To the left is the recording seat, and to the right is the press seat. The track and field area is in the east, with athlete rest tents on both sides of the chairman's stand. The ball game field is in the south. The circumference is the track and field track. The outer circumference is entirely spectator stands. More than 180 male and female disciplinary squad members maintain order in the field. Outside, there are two companies of infantry and one squad of mounted police from the Provincial Government Guard Regiment, with extremely tight security.

Number of Athletes: A total of twenty-seven schools participated. Those in Jinan are: Provincial Commercial Middle School, First Normal School, First Women's Normal School, First Rural Normal School, First Middle School, First Girls' Middle School, First Vocational Girls' Vocational School, People's Education School, Zhengyi Middle School, Yuying Middle School, Donglu Middle School, Aimei Middle School, Third Experimental Elementary School, totaling fourteen schools. Those in various counties are: Provincial Dongchang Second Middle School, Taian Third Middle School, Linyi Fifth Middle School, Caozhou Sixth Middle School, Jining Seventh Middle School, Qingzhou Tenth Middle School, Qufu Second Normal School, Qingzhou Fourth Normal School, Jining Third Vocational School, Ziyang Fifth Vocational School, Changqing Middle School, Weixian Middle School, Yanshan Middle School, totaling thirteen schools. Those who registered but did not arrive: Dongchang Third Normal School, Linqing Second Vocational School. As for Linqing Eleventh Middle School, a urgent letter arrived yesterday stating that due to local unrest, they could not come. The principal of Huimin Fourth Middle School is in Jinan and said that the school's students have arrived at Xingjiadu north of the Yellow River, but the troops on the south bank do not allow them to cross the river, so they did not arrive yesterday. Director He of the Education Department promised to send a telegram to the troops stationed there to quickly allow the students to cross the river, but they still could not come to Jinan today. The original number of track and field athletes was 458, but due to the non-arrival of the above four schools, the total number who arrived was 435.

Attendees: Chairman He Siyuan (Director of the Education Department), Honorary Vice-Chairmen Yu Enbo (Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mining), Chen Mingyu (Director of the Department of Industry and Commerce), Zhu Xi (Director of the Department of Civil Affairs), Chen Luanshu (Director of the Department of Construction), Yuan Jiapu (Director of the Department of Finance), Zhang Jinjian (Training Director of the Provincial Rectification Committee), and representatives from other agencies, all staff of the sports meet, etc.

Opening Ceremony: The ceremony started as scheduled at 10:00 AM. Chief Commander Zhang Yiguang, Chairman He Siyuan presided over and delivered the opening speech, which briefly stated: Fellow comrades, fellow students, fellow athletes, we are holding the first provincial middle school joint sports meet here today. Know that this is not for individual sports, but for the entire Chinese nation's sports. Our Chinese nation has a history of 4,000 years. Recently, our culture has fallen behind and our politics are oppressed. The biggest reason is that the nation is not competitive. The reason why the nation is not competitive is because it lacks team spirit and team morality. This meeting is to show the development of the entire Chinese national spirit and the development of the entire Chinese national morality. It is not about one victory or defeat. It is about uniting and going on. This is the expression of the development of the national spirit. Understand this, and you will know that victory is not worth celebrating and defeat is not worth shame. The main idea of today's meeting is like this.

Next, Vice-Chairman Yuan Jiapu delivered a training speech on behalf of the provincial government, which briefly stated: Today, students are here for a meeting, not for individual sports, but for national sports. Because our Chinese nation does not exercise regularly, it gradually becomes weak, leading to internal and external troubles, and cannot enjoy freedom, equality, and happiness. If this continues, it will not only lead to national subjugation but also extermination. Therefore, sports and nationalism have a direct and great relationship. Next, Zhang Jinjian, training director of the Provincial Rectification Committee, gave a training speech. After the speech, photos were taken, and the parade began.

News

Qingdao University President and Funding Confirmed

President Yang Zhensheng... Annual Funding of 480,000 Yuan

(Jinan Correspondence) The preparation of National Qingdao University has been going on for a year, but due to various difficulties, it has not been established and started school. This time, at the National Education Conference held in Beijing, education figures gathered and all agreed that the establishment of Qingda University should not be delayed. It was initially decided that Yang Zhensheng would be the president of Qingda University. The preparation of everything has been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that Mr. Yang is a native of Penglai, Shandong Province, a graduate of Peking University, and a graduate of Columbia University in the United States. He is currently the director of the liberal arts department of Tsinghua in Beiping. Yesterday, the provincial government received a telegram from Beijing stating that the National Government had officially announced Yang as the president of Qingda University. After Yang finishes his work at Tsinghua in Beiping, he will go to Qingdao to start preparations. It is heard that school can be started after the summer vacation. The university's budget has been approved by the Ministry of Education's administrative meeting, with an annual funding of about 480,000 yuan. The source of funding is 360,000 yuan from the Shandong Provincial Government in the 19th year [of the Republic] (including 80,000 yuan for start-up expenses), 36,000 yuan from the Qingdao Municipal Government annually, and 12,000 yuan annually from the Jiaoji Railway. The original amount was 30,000 yuan, but it was reduced to 12,000 yuan due to Japanese accountants interfering. The remaining 80,000 to 90,000 yuan will be allocated by the central government. The university has decided to first establish colleges of arts and sciences. The education department has decided to establish a department in Jinan to train rural normal school teachers. Qingda University has decided to run a summer school in Qingdao during this year's summer vacation, summoning a portion of the education bureau chiefs, county supervisors, and elementary school teachers from all 107 counties in the province, as well as all elementary school teachers in Qingdao, to the school for training. Party and state dignitaries such as Cai Yuanpei will also come to the school to give lectures. All the teachers of the summer school have been hired by Yang Zhensheng in Beijing.

A Review of the Second National Education Conference (V)

(V) Plan to Improve Elementary Education

(I) Principles

(1) All regulations should take the lowest limits and the most economical expenses;

(2) In addition to the must-be-uniform, pay attention to flexibility.

(II) Establishment

(1) Elementary schools and kindergartens should be established by municipalities in principle. The central government and provinces should share subsidies;

(2) The division of school districts should be consistent with local autonomous regions in principle;

(3) Neighborhoods, towns, villages, private individuals, and private legal entities can establish elementary schools and kindergartens. Municipal and county governments should provide subsidies;

(4) In principle, one elementary school and kindergarten should be established in each neighborhood in the city;

(5) Each county and city should set up nurseries according to local needs;

(6) The Ministry of Education should formulate standards for the establishment of elementary schools and kindergartens. Provincial and municipal special city bureaus should formulate the minimum standards for the establishment of elementary schools and kindergartens;

(7) Set up by people of completely Chinese nationality, employing people of completely Chinese nationality as teachers and staff.

(III) Funding

(1) Designated local funding should be organized and guaranteed. For deficiencies, the Ministry of Education should stipulate methods to expand funding;

(2) In the start-up costs of elementary schools and kindergartens, the ratio of construction equipment to regular expenses should be 6 to 4, or 7 to 3 in principle. Regular expenses should be determined as the annual fee for each class of students or each student. Salaries and wages should account for at most 80 percent, the cost of purchasing books should account for 2 to 3 percent, and the reserve fund should account for 2 to 5 percent. The standards should be formulated by the provinces and cities and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval;

(3) The accounting methods and property management methods of elementary schools and kindergartens should be stipulated by the Ministry of Education in outline, and the provincial and municipal bureaus should formulate implementation methods and submit them to the Ministry of Education for approval;

(4) The Ministry of Education should formulate detailed implementation methods for the custody of elementary schools and kindergartens, public disclosure methods, and property transfer methods, and submit them to the Ministry of Education for approval.

(IV) Construction Equipment

(1) The Ministry of Education should formulate model drawings for various school building constructions (including lighting, ventilation, area, school site selection, and school layout). The provinces and cities should select several types as the local school building standards;

(2) The Ministry of Education should formulate various school building rating scales for provinces, cities, and counties to use as standards for improving school buildings;

(3) The Ministry of Education should formulate various model drawings for tables and chairs. The provinces and cities should select several types as the local table and chair standards;

(4) The Ministry of Education should formulate equipment rating scales for provinces, cities, and counties to use as standards for improving equipment;

(5) The provincial education departments should formulate styles based on the actual status of common equipment in elementary schools and kindergartens in the province and use them as standards for cities and counties to adopt;

(6) The Ministry of Education should investigate the forms currently used by elementary schools and kindergartens across the country and stipulate simple forms for provinces and cities to adopt;

(7) The provincial and municipal governments should follow the principles established in the school health implementation plan promulgated by the Ministries of Education and Health, and carefully detail the standards for various health, disease prevention, sports, games, and other equipment, and earnestly implement them.

(V) Teachers and Staff

(1) The Ministry of Education should stipulate an outline of the inspection standards, and the provincial and municipal authorities should stipulate detailed methods and set up an inspection committee to handle them. The regulations of the inspection committee should be stipulated by the Ministry of Education;

(2) All current teachers and staff should be given a one-year license. Those who obtain a license three times in a row for three years should be given a ten-year license. Those who have made significant progress should be given a lifetime license. Those who do not make progress should still be given a one-year license. Those who do not make progress after obtaining a one-year license three times in a row should have their licenses revoked.
